< review>
DO NOT USE THIS COMPANY!

I received a mailer from Secure One showing a promising rate for a refi, so I bit at the chance of saving some money.  I started the process in early March.  They were very responsive and willing in the beginning to gather all of my information.  After our initial discussions, their response time dropped from daily responses to taking 3-5 days to respond to an email or phone call.  At this point, I figured it was a fraudulent operation and they managed to just collect all of my personal information for identity theft.  However, after nearly 2 months (during which I sent numerous follow-up emails), I was finally informed the loan was close to closing, and I received the final closing disclosure, thinking the end was in sight!   But then earlier this week, I was told my loan was not going to be processed because the lock they made at the beginning was "improperly" entered into their system, and since current rates are much higher than the locked rate, their investors would not accept the loan at this rate.  What's the point of a lock if they don't hold it!?  Not only are these ethics despicable, but probably illegal based upon the loan estimate and loan disclosure showing these promised rates.  And because I chose to go with Secure One, I missed out on a low rate with a reputable company.  Don't even consider going with them.  Use a real company that you can trust.< /review>

< review>
One of the worst and saltiest meals ever. After waiting 35 minutes after ordering the waitress came by and asked if we would like some bread. There was salt on the butter! I ordered the soup of the day - cream of summer squash. I could barely eat any of it and would not have gone past the first spoonful if I hadn't been starving from waiting almost an hour. Yes we were a party of 10 but when we came in there was hardly anyone one else in the restaurant. All I could taste was salt, salt and more salt. My lips were literally burning from the salt. Not realizing my soup would be all salt and no flavor, I had ordered a side of the garlic fries. Guess what - too salty to eat. Someone needs to tell the chef that there are other flavors in the world. You can always add more at the table if you like, but unless they have invented a salt remover, there's no way to get rid of it once the chef with dead taste buds has dumped a pound and a half in. This is the second time I have had to eat at this place as part of a company function and both times my food was inedible. I worked in gourmet houses for much of my early life - I know what good food tastes like - this ain't it! And I wasn't alone in my opinion. Nearly everyone at the table complained about how salty their burgers were. Can't believe this place stays in business.</review>

<user_name>Brian Loos< /user_name><userid>115607878971174768092</userid>< pictures>
None< /pictures>
< review>
I visited the assembly last night with my brother and friend and we all thoroughly enjoyed the experience. We order the garlic parmesan  fries and scotch olives as an appetizers and were very impressed. Even though these are just simple bar food type items, we really enjoyed them. We asked for some aioli to dip the fries in, which was no mistake. If you want to get the fries, I would highly recommend asking for aioli with them as well. Moving on to dinner, we ordered a goat cheese and quinoa fritter salad, the seared seasonal seafood, and the Manhattan fillet steak. I had the goat cheese and quinoa fritters. Although, I would not recommend them unless you really like goat cheese. I only tried bites of the steak and halibut, but they were both really good. Dessert is where Assembly looses a star for me. My friend described it as "sick and wrong", but I have to disagree with her. The sorbets were very, very sour, but I really liked the flavors. They were light and refreshing; exactly what a sorbet should be.

EDIT:
Took away a star aftera  return visit during restaurant week. While nothing was bad, but the presentation felt sloppy and the entrees were underwhelming. The meat board and fried cheese curds were good, but not good enough to maintain the four stars I had originally posted.</review>

<Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMIj6g8mytTAw6pJoDCmQ0EJIoclbXSzX99OMYQ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMluJ2MgkhxG1q0r6Hz7PhRBuz3erFgfy5EuIHA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNGaX3ojaUUKW0lt22bKdoUTAfDwJit0k0NFSgR=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pictures><Resp>None</Resp><gmapID>0x808fbf4586a24f11:0xc4961b13e9ba7778< /gmapID></record></dataset><record>
<gmapID>0x808fbf4586a24f11:0xc4961b13e9ba7778< /gmapID><Date>1570299184463</Date>< review>
Since my daughter gets crazy about BTS, she starts to like Korean food also, so we got to try all the Korean restaurants in the area. We've seen this one in the Lion Supermarket shopping center for a long time now, we tried it and went there a few times already.
Korean restaurants prices are mostly higher than Chinese or other ethnic food as I (payer) notice for the same quality and quantity. I think Korean food is more complex to prepare or just catered to Koreans who are accustomed to high prices.
The food is mostly spices and tasty in its own way. The home made noodles are quite chewy and the sauce is quite tasty, although they're just flour, my daughter love them for some reasons.
I and my wife like the hot and spicy seafood soup, which is great for when you're under the weather, will sweat after a hot bowl of soup and rice, quite tasty, easy to eat.
My son likes the Kimchi fried rice which I don't really care for, but as long as he enjoys it, it's fine to me.
The chap chae, Korean famous glass noodles are OK IMO, I can do better at home but it's OK to try.
Everyone likes all the little dishes of pickles that served in most Korean restaurants.
This place is quite clean and the service is excellent, all dishes are over $11 as I recalled which is not terribly expensive but for what we get, is a little overpriced. Anyhow, it's the taste that counts and as long as everyone in the family not complaining and finish their food.
So, this will be our regular Korean restaurant when we have the urge for some spicy food, all 4 thumbs up.< /review>

<GmapID>0x80d954b522b0826b:0xa2298f8b840076d1< /GmapID><rating>1<//rating><Resp>None<//Resp>< review>
(Summary: Bottom line is that the service with Express is not good. The case is now closed and the credit card company decided to recharge the fine Express tried to charge me for.
I d also like to inform readers that some of the reviews given here are written by employees from Express. You can check that out yourself on the internet. Most 5-star reviews here are traceable from Express!)

I rented a car here November, 2014, for 500USD (actually more than the price claimed on their website, but still one of the cheaper around San DIego).

The pickup service at San Diego Airport was nice. The car I got to rent was however not (completely bumped, making bad noises when braking), but maybe I could not expect more for the money.
I returned the car already after 1 out of 4 weeks, because I did not have to use it anymore and did not have a parking lot available for it. Express did not want to give me any refund, nor accepted the car when I wanted to return it without a completely filled tank. Although this is not very customer friendly, with me returning the car so early, I could still not complain until this point because this was something I had agreed on in the contract. My experiences so far however did make me not wanting to return to them in future.

Bigger problems started to arise after I returned the car. I got a mail from Express that I committed a toll violation in the LA region. They kindly informed me that they already paid for it, charged my credit card, and charged me a fine in addition for having been outside San Diego County. I had never agreed to pay for the ticket however.

Express could have known I had never been in LA: I only had driven 80 miles with the car, the place where the ''crime'' was committed being further away. Irrespective of that, they paid the ticket (taking away my right and possibility to dispute it!) and charged me a fine for having been outside San Diego County on top (60 dollar for the violation ticket, 100 dollar for having been outside SD County). This 100 dollar shows the incompetence of Express again: even if the car had been outside SD County, the 100 dollar that they charged me is based on nothing: according to the contract, a penalty of 25 cents per mile is given for driving outside SD. 100 dollar would mean 400 miles. I however only drove 80 miles with the car...... (which is in the contract, so Express knew about that).<//review>

<text>What an experience!! The guys at go jump are super professional but fun and light hearted at the same time. At no point was I concerned about my safety or well being. We went as a group of 5, we pre booked online and once we got there it was a smooth check in process. We booked our jump for 2pm and were harnessed and ready to jump within half hour of our jump time. You have the option of paying extra for hand cam footage OR having an extra diver jump with you filming the entire jump for you. ($98 for hand cam & $128 for the extra diver). The jump itself was phenomenal. Seeing the ocean and skyline was absolutely breathtaking!! It was about 5ish mins in total. Be prepared to have a bit of ear pain on the decent, but once your ears pop your good to go!

I would definitely recommend this place to anyone interested in going skydiving. You're in good hands at go jump!<//text>< pictures>

We had such a great time skydiving with GoJump Oceanside!! I went with my mom, brother, and friend who was the only person in our group who had completed a jump before. Our original booking was for a Sunday, however we weren‚Äôt able to jump because of the marine layer, which was still thick at 3pm. We rescheduled for 2 days later at 1pm. We arrived at 12:45pm and ended up jumping at 6:00pm. This was because of the same marine layer issue and it being a semi cloudy day. The staff were very friendly and great with keeping us informed and honest with their predictions on if there were going to be jumps that day. We ate lunch and spent most of our time at the humane society next door (and even adopted and took home a cat ü§∑üèº‚Äç‚ôÄÔ∏è) after we got the call we were suited up and in the air within 45 min. My instructor, Matt, was knowledgeable, safe, and made sure I was comfortable starting on the ground before we boarded the plane all the way until we were back on the ground after the jump! These guys don't know anything.  I am a C license skydiver with over 350 jumps and was told since I had only made 7 jumps in the past 12 months and not 12 jumps in 12 months that I was not current.  Clearly they don't know the currency requirements in section 5 of USPA SIM that C and D license jumpers need to make at least 1 jump every 180 days to stay current. If you are looking to travel to DZ's outside of your home DZ stay away from this company.  Rude and does not even know the rules in which they operate under. Beware - unprofessional staff, rude and arrogant! I skydived here around mid-Jan 2020 and my tandem skydiver, JC, was extremely rude, arrogant, condescending, and impatient. He made several cocky and snide remarks, and was very impatient at explaining basic procedures to me. When I asked him to repeat something since he was talking too fast, he replied something to the effect of "why don't you look here instead of listening". That is just one account of his misbehaviour. In short, if I were to make an analogy, he was one of those people who looks at you up-down, sizes you up, and then decides on the appropriate tone of voice and demeanor to direct at you.

I actually feel sorry for such people. In their conduct, they reveal how full of anger, fear, and insecurity they are deep down inside. Any individual who is grateful for life and humble would never behave in this manner...

Besides him, even in general, the staff is extremely unprofessional. They're basically young people (not that I have anything against young people. Also, JC mentioned above was much older, by the way) who have not been given training in customer service, how to behave and conduct themselves in front of clients, etc. I heard several of their staff regularly using the F-word and making misogynistic comments. Some of their customers had come there with the families and little children, so I'm sure they would have found such conduct objectionable as well.

After a jump, I also overheard the staff discussing technicalities of skydiving (which apparently were not performed well-enough the last time), which does not inspire confidence among customers who are right there listening to all that.

Finally, I paid extra to have my video edited and in the video they sent me, my voice is not audible and there is background music playing over it...

All in all, a very bad experience. Ruined my whole day. I had to go for dinner in the evening after the skydiving, and didn't even enjoy myself there because of the horrible skydiving experience.

If you're planning to go here, I would advise you to avoid JC as your tandem skydiver at all costs! Or better yet, I would avoid this place altogether...<//Text>

<Pics>None<//Pics><response>{'time': 1558875973334, 'text': "Hi Ashley,\nFirst off we would like to thank you for wanting to jump with us in the first place. Skydiving is an incredible sport and our goal is to share that with as many people as possible with a safe and incredible experience! Unfortunately, there are a few things that effect the safety of our favorite outdoor sport that are beyond our control- weather is one of them. Transition seasons (spring and fall) can sometimes bring a marine layer that will sit over the water and can move in and sit on top of our airspace making it unsafe to jump. Sometimes it clears up within minutes, sometimes it comes in and out, sometimes it sits there all day. Because the marine layer depends on outside versus water temperatures, they aren't on weather radars as clouds and can be very hard to predict or track. We do our absolute best to keep each of our customers informed as soon as we make decisions based on weather. Sometimes we nail it but other times the weather does something we didn't predict. Unfortunately those days you picked to jump, the weather wasn't operational. We do our best to let you guys know as soon as we know what's going on but sometimes we don't predict fast enough and I extend our apologizes for that. We know it can be frustrating to have your hopes set on jumping, make plans and organize travel to have weather stand in your way. We promise that if we could control it, it would be sunny all day long! :) On your rescheduled day we pushed your time back because the clouds were in and out all day and we landed a few airplanes without even dropping the jumpers. At a certain point, the clouds came back in and never went back out and that's when we inform all the customers. < review>
Three words to describe GoJump: Careless, thoughtless and incompetent. Not a great combination for a sky diving business.

Similar to others' experience, their operation is poorly run with no customer service: they basically could give two flying you-know-what about the customer. I'll give it to them that they did so with a smile.

We booked a reservation, left work early, drove two hours from OC and arrived 15 minutes before our schedule appointment. When we arrived, they told us that the wait was 2.5 hours. They have our email and phone number and it didn't occur to them to let us know. The fog kept rolling in and they still encouraged patrons to "wait and see another 30 minutes", it was dusk by then and they had two more planes to go up.  I figure if this is a well established, expert shop, they would at least understand weather trends and let their appointments know that the jumps have been pushed back and begin your reschedule people. We understood weather is unpredictable and safety is the number one priority. But that does not give a business the excuse to operate in a fashion where they clearly do not care about the customer or their time. Needless to say, they called the day and we never went up. We wasted 5 hours and a half of tank of gas (plus tolls).<//review>

< name>

< review>
All safety measures and precautions are taken, so there is no complaint about that from me. I appreciate that they don't take risks with safety. However, as many of the other reviews have mentioned, GoJump does not value the customer's time. They canceled our first appointment without notifying us, and we only found out after making the long drive down to the area. We rescheduled twice after that, and they were extremely inflexible about times. We had booked our first reservation about a month in advance, so they should have been more accommodating with their times.

The third reservation we booked was at 5 pm.  Remember, the time is booked with the assumption that you're actually going to be getting on the plane pretty soon after that time. We called at 3 to confirm that they were still on, and all seemed well. We arrived at 4:45 pm to be told that there was a 2 hour delay. We waited for an hour and 20 minutes, and then they canceled the rest of the jumps due to weather. There was no compensation for our wait, drive, or the inconvenience of constantly rescheduling.

Again, I'm glad that they don't try to force jumps in bad weather conditions, but this inefficient scheduling is ridiculous. I can't imagine trying to do this on a vacation with limited time. If you're really set on using this company, I'd suggest to book your reservation in the middle of the day and then plan to make it a full-day commitment.

When we finally did get to jump, it was truly an amazing experience. The tandem pilots are great and seem really focused on making sure you're comfortable.

In all, I think the office should be more organized and helpful. I think the best way to ensure your jump the first time is to schedule it for late morning or early afternoon. Thank you.</review>

<Text>If it is your first time going skydiving and you would like to tandem skydive, I would recommend buying your ticket on Groupon. It is much cheaper. They are very nice people. It is usually somewhat crowded but the wait to go up is 30 minutes or less. The planes are always taking off to drop a new load of sky divers. They fully answer any questions you have and have great package deals for those who love skydiving. The area is calm. However, parking isn't that great. They also sell food outside while you wait. If you just want to watch, they have an area outside to watch.
Now when you go on the plane, they take you over the ocean. The instructors have GoPros to record every moment.
Appointments are required to secure your spot. They will cancel and reschedule due to weather. Make sure you check the weather if you don't wish to get an email or a call about them having to reschedule due to the weather.<//Text>< Date>

<Text>Some friends and I made a reservation for a sunset jump (4pm), and drove out from las vegas to do it.  We left Vegas at 7 am, ready to go and with plenty of time to arrive, book our hotel, and head to skydive.  We got a text at 1 pm that day saying that our dive was canceled due to unforeseen circumstances.  We called, and were told that weather had pushed the timetable back, and if we wanted to come down they would try to fit us in, but no guarantees.

We decided to try our luck, and drove down...

We arrived at the office, and asked to speak to someone about whether we would be able to fly or not, they directed us to the manager who told us that at 8 am it had gotten very cloudy, and no one was able to jump for 3 hours.  As such the timetable had been pushed back, and sadly there was no time for us to jump today.  I explained we had driven all the way out from Las Vegas to jump with them, and he told us he understood that but there was nothing he could do, he offered to reschedule us for another day, but as they were full both Saturday and Sunday he was unwilling to schedule us for then.

The reasons for the low review score are these.

1.  The company did not call/text us when inclement weather occured to let us know we might be delayed.  Nor did they let us know after it was clear we WOULD be canceled (at 11 am)  They waited until 1pm to let us know.  I completely understand if things get canceled because of weather and am in no way holding them responsible for the weather.

2.  The company was unwilling to work with us in any way shape or form after bumping us from our times.  A reservation is a reservation, if someone has one for a specific time it holds no less value than someone from an earlier time.  If they are going to bump people who are later in favor of those who are earlier then it makes no sense whatsoever to EVER book later with these people.

3.  The company was perfectly willing to cancel later reservations, yet was unwilling to push anyone from other days in order to make things right with those who were canceled in prior days.

4.  While the manager displayed a calm demeanor, the receptionists don't.  They are rude, and unpleasant.

5.  If you say "I would like to make this right for you"  then do nothing whatsoever to "make this right for you"  then it is a lie.  Don't lie to potential customers.

We booked with Lake Elsinore skydiving the next day and had an awesome time.  its a little bit more spendy, but the customer service was good, and it actually felt like they cared.</Text><Pictures>None< /Pictures><Resp>None<//Resp>< Gmap_id>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
GoJumpOceanside. The only complaint I have was that we had an appointment on Sunday at 12pm and we didn't jump till right before 5pm. When we arrived and checked in they said they hadn't jumped anyone all morning due to weather(sky's weren't clear enough over head) and said we had a 2hr wait , they started to send planes up but they had all the morning appointment to get through and catch up on, so we left and went to go eat, came back at 2pm and still had more of wait and they were stoping again because clouds were coming back.But to be honest after being there you could say that they should call you and let you know what's happening if delayed and your appointment is in the PM but in reality they only had 2office staff their that day and that's a lot of people to call and no one can detect the what the weather is going to do. And to be honest I'd rather wait all day or reschedule if their major concern is the safety of everyone going into the sky , so for me I'd rather be delayed hours if it means it's the best safety precautions they can do by delaying and making sure the weather is in good condition to sky dive . But anyways it Was a great experience! , the skydive was nothing like I thought it would be! IT WAS AWESOME! -and my sky dive Professional Thomas made it awesome! The only complaint is the delayed hours but after going through it , it was completely understandable weather safety is serious and I'd rather have that then a business that doesn't care about that, and Go Jump Oceanside is by the beach so you have to realize that , that kind of weather is a common thing their so delays are highly possible. And since we were delayed about 4.5 hrs when we jumped it was sunset time so that was even better . So my advice is if your going their plan an appointment around from morning time to 1pm and for sure you probably will jump that day even with delays ,. And plan it to be an all day thing or half day event , don't just plan on coming in at your time and being out in an hour but other than that it was a AWESOME EXPERIENCE and I would do it again<//review>
